§ 152.01 MAINTENANCE; RESPONSIBILITY.
   The maintenance of trees and shrubs located upon a right-of-way is, and
shall remain, the duty of the owner of the adjacent property.
(2013 Code, Title V, Ch. 7, § 1) (Ord. III-D-1-a(1), passed - -; Ord. III-D-2-a
(3), passed 11- -1994; Ord. passed 7-13-1998)
§ 152.02 SHADE TREES.
   All shade trees within the town or near any public street or alley in said
town, shall be kept trimmed so that the lowest branch of each tree shall be at
a distance from the level of the street or alley along which such tree or trees
of not less than eight feet and that the owner or owners of the land on which
such trees stand shall be and they are hereby required to keep such trees so
trimmed to comply with this subchapter.
(2013 Code, Title V, Ch. 7, § 2) (Ord. III-D-1-a(1), passed - -; Ord. III-D-2-a
(3), passed 11- -1994; Ord. passed 7-13-1998)
§ 152.03 NOTIFICATION.
   (A)   Should any person whose land abuts any street or alley in said town
fail to trim his or her trees so as to cause same to comply with this
subchapter, it shall be the duty of the Marshal of said town, upon approval of
the Town Council so to do, to notify the owner to at once trim up such tree or
trees to comply herewith, that should such owner fail, neglect or refuse to
comply with such notice within ten days from time of receiving same, that such
Marshal shall have, and he or she hereby is granted authority to trim such
trees as to cause same to comply with this subchapter.
(2013 Code, Title V, Ch. 7, § 3)
   (B)   Whenever any property owner of the town shall become aware of an
unsafe condition caused by a tree or shrub located upon the right-of-way of the
town, said property owner should notify the town immediately in order that the
town can take corrective action by the removal of said dangerous condition.
(2013 Code, Title V, Ch. 7, § 4)
(Ord. III-D-1-a(1), passed - -; Ord. III-D-2-a(3), passed 11- -1994; Ord.
passed 7-13-1998)
§ 152.04 INDEX OF TREES.
   The town shall establish an index of trees which property owners have
requested to be trimmed or removed for cosmetic or maintenance reasons, and to
the extent possible, budgeting funds for the removal of said trees based upon a
need basis as established by a priority list prepared by the Town Street
Superintendent and/or Town Manager, and at the discretion of the Town Council.
Each property owner shall be responsible for 50% of the cost of maintaining or
removing of said tree or shrub, and the Town Council shall pay the remaining
50% of the costs incurred in maintaining or removing said tree or shrub.
(2013 Code, Title V, Ch. 7, § 5) (Ord. III-D-1-a(1), passed - -; Ord. III-D-2-a
(3), passed 11- -1994; Ord. passed 7-13-1998; Ord. 2018-10-8(D), passed 10-8-
2018)
§ 152.05 LIEN.
   The moneys advanced by the Town Council shall become a lien upon the real
estate and shall be assessed and collectible as are property taxes of the
subject land owner.
(2013 Code, Title V, Ch. 7, § 6) (Ord. III-D-1-a(1), passed - -; Ord. III-D-2-a
(3), passed 11- -1994; Ord. passed 7-13-1998; Ord. 2018-10-8(D), passed 10-8-
2018)
§ 152.06 REPLANTING; FEE.
   (A)   All replanting made as a result of trees removed under this subchapter
shall be chosen by the Street Superintendent and/or Town Manager.
(2013 Code, Title V, Ch. 7, § 7)
   (B)   The town will pay up to $300 for each tree replanted, with the
remainder to be paid by the property owner.
(2013 Code, Title V, Ch. 7, § 8)
